This taint effect:\n\n1. **Prevents new pods from being scheduled** on the node (like `NoSchedule`)\n2. **Removes the node from Service EndpointSlices** - traffic won't be routed to the node\n3. **Does NOT evict existing pods** (unlike `NoExecute`)\n\n## Key Characteristics\n\n| Feature | NoSchedule | NoScheduleNoTraffic | NoExecute |\n|---------|-----------|-------------------|-----------|\n| Prevents Scheduling | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |\n| Removes from Load Balancer | ✗ | ✓ | ✓ |\n| Evicts Pods | ✗ | ✗ | ✓ |\n| Pod Tolerance Respected | ✓ | ✓ | ✓ |\n\n## Implementation Files\n\n### Patch Files\n\nThe implementation is provided as a series of patch files:\n\n1. **0001-add-noschedulenotraffic-constant.patch**\n   - Adds the `TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic` constant to the API types\n   - Updates comments to mention the new taint effect\n\n2. **0002-update-taint-validation.patch**\n   - Updates taint validation functions to accept the new effect\n   - Applies to both `pkg/util/taints` and kubectl\n\n3. **0003-update-scheduler-filter.patch**\n   - Updates the scheduler's filter function to include NoScheduleNoTraffic\n   - Ensures pods can't be scheduled on tainted nodes without tolerations\n\n4. **0004-update-endpointslice.patch**\n   - Updates the endpoint slice controller to exclude nodes with the taint\n   - Prevents traffic from being routed to tainted nodes\n\n5. **0005-update-tests.patch**\n   - Adds test cases for the new taint effect\n\n### Documentation Files\n\n- **IMPLEMENTATION_CHANGES.md**: Detailed explanation of each code change required\n- **IMPLEMENTATION_PLAN.md**: Overview of changes needed across the codebase\n\n## How to Apply\n\n### Option 1: Using Git Patches\n\n```bash\n# Navigate to your Kubernetes repository root\ncd /path/to/kubernetes\n\n# Apply patches in order\ngit apply 0001-add-noschedulenotraffic-constant.patch\ngit apply 0002-update-taint-validation.patch\ngit apply 0003-update-scheduler-filter.patch\ngit apply 0004-update-endpointslice.patch\ngit apply 0005-update-tests.patch\n```\n\n### Option 2: Manual Application\n\nFollow the detailed instructions in **IMPLEMENTATION_CHANGES.md** to manually apply the changes to each file.\n\n## Implementation Details\n\n### 1. API Type Definition\n**File**: `staging/src/k8s.io/api/core/v1/types.go`\n\nThe new taint effect constant is added to the TaintEffect type:\n\n```go\nconst (\n    TaintEffectNoSchedule TaintEffect = \"NoSchedule\"\n    TaintEffectPreferNoSchedule TaintEffect = \"PreferNoSchedule\"\n    TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic TaintEffect = \"NoScheduleNoTraffic\"\n    TaintEffectNoExecute TaintEffect = \"NoExecute\"\n)\n```\n\n### 2. Validation Updates\n**Files**:\n- `pkg/util/taints/taints.go`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/kubectl/pkg/cmd/taint/utils.go`\n\nThe `validateTaintEffect()` function is updated to accept the new effect.\n\n### 3. Scheduler Filter\n**File**: `pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/helper/taint.go`\n\nThe `DoNotScheduleTaintsFilterFunc()` is updated to include NoScheduleNoTraffic:\n\n```go\nreturn t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoSchedule ||\n       t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoScheduleNoTraffic ||\n       t.Effect == v1.TaintEffectNoExecute\n```\n\nThis ensures the scheduler applies the same pod tolerance checking for NoScheduleNoTraffic as it does for NoSchedule and NoExecute.\n\n### 4. EndpointSlice Controller\n**Files**:\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/utils.go`\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/reconciler.go`\n\nThe endpoint slice controller is updated to:\n- Check if a node has the NoScheduleNoTraffic taint\n- Exclude pods on tainted nodes from service endpoints\n- Respect the `PublishNotReadyAddresses` service setting\n\n### 5. Node Controller\n**File**: `pkg/controller/nodelifecycle/node_lifecycle_controller.go`\n\nNo changes needed - the node controller only evicts pods for NoExecute taints.\n\n## Testing\n\n### Run Full Test Suite\n```bash\nmake test\n```\n\n### Run Specific Test Files\n```bash\n# Scheduler plugin tests\ngo test ./pkg/scheduler/framework/plugins/helper/... -v\n\n# Endpoint slice tests\ngo test ./staging/src/k8s.io/endpointslice/...  -v\n\n# Taint utility tests\ngo test ./pkg/util/taints/... -v\n```\n\n### Verification Steps\n\n1. Verify that a pod with a matching toleration can be scheduled on a node with NoScheduleNoTraffic taint\n2. Verify that a pod without a matching toleration CANNOT be scheduled on the tainted node\n3. Verify that pods already running on a node are NOT evicted when the taint is added\n4. Verify that endpoints for a service do NOT include pods on nodes with NoScheduleNoTraffic taint\n5. Verify that traffic from a service is NOT routed to tainted nodes\n\n## Use Cases\n\n1. **Rolling Node Updates**: Add NoScheduleNoTraffic to a node before updating it. This prevents new pods from being scheduled and removes it from load balancing while allowing existing pods to gracefully terminate.\n\n2. **Node Maintenance**: Mark a node for maintenance without evicting running workloads immediately.\n\n3. **Gradual Decommissioning**: Prepare a node for removal without disrupting running services.\n\n4. **Custom Workload Management**: Allow applications to implement custom eviction logic while still preventing new pods and traffic.\n\n## Backward Compatibility\n\nThis change is fully backward compatible:\n- Existing taints (NoSchedule, NoExecute, PreferNoSchedule) continue to work as before\n- The new taint effect is opt-in - users must explicitly add it\n- No changes to pod scheduling or eviction behavior for existing taints\n\n## Related Configuration\n\nPods can tolerate the NoScheduleNoTraffic taint like any other taint:\n\n```yaml\napiVersion: v1\nkind: Pod\nmetadata:\n  name: example-pod\nspec:\n  tolerations:\n  - key: \"node-being-updated\"\n    operator: \"Equal\"\n    value: \"true\"\n    effect: \"NoScheduleNoTraffic\"\n  containers:\n  - name: nginx\n    image: nginx\n```\n\n## Additional Resources\n\n- [Kubernetes Taints and Tolerations](https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/scheduling-eviction/taint-and-toleration/)\n- [Kubernetes EndpointSlices](https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/services-networking/endpoint-slices/)\n- [Kubernetes Scheduler](https://kubernetes.io/docs/concepts/scheduling-eviction/kube-scheduler/)\n\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":0,"cache_creation_input_tokens":695,"cache_read_input_tokens":115166,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":695},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"efddb694-7196-4db1-9902-9a62eb332ddb","uuid":"25c748f8-9c68-4b19-881e-e05bcc154735"}
